(h) Interim Interest. If the Issuing Lender for any LeÔŅĹer of Credit shall make any LC Disbursement, then, unless the Borrower shall reimburse such LC Disbursement in full on the date such LC Disbursement is made, the unpaid amount thereof shall bear interest, for each day from and including the date such LC Disbursement is made to, but excluding the date that the Borrower reimburses such LC Disbursement, at the rate per annum then applicable to Syndicated ABR Loans; provided that, if the Borrower fails to reimburse such LC Disbursement when due pursuant to paragraph (f) of this SecÔŅĹon 2.06, then SecÔŅĹon 2.13(e) shall apply.  Interest accrued pursuant to this paragraph shall be for the account of such Issuing Lender, except that interest accrued on and aÔŅĹer the date of payment by any Lender pursuant to paragraph (e) of this SecÔŅĹon 2.06 to reimburse such Issuing Lender shall be for the account of such Lender to the extent of such payment, and shall be payable on demand or, if no demand has been made, on the date on which the Borrower reimburses the applicable LC Disbursement in full. 

(i) AddiÔŅĹonal Issuing Lenders; TerminaÔŅĹon of Issuing Lenders.  An Issuing Lender may be added, or an exisÔŅĹng Issuing Lender may be terminated, under this Agreement at any ÔŅĹme by wriÔŅĹen agreement between the Borrower, the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent and the applicable new or terminated Issuing Lender (which agreement shall, in the case of any new Issuing Lender, set forth the LC Sublimit Share thereof).  The AdministraÔŅĹve Agent shall noÔŅĹfy the Lenders of any such addiÔŅĹon or terminaÔŅĹon.  At the ÔŅĹme any such terminaÔŅĹon shall become effecÔŅĹve, the Borrower shall pay all unpaid fees accrued for the account of the Issuing Lender being terminated pursuant to SecÔŅĹon 2.12(b).  From and aÔŅĹer the effecÔŅĹve date of any such addiÔŅĹon, the 

new Issuing Lender shall have all the rights and obligaÔŅĹons of an Issuing Lender under this Agreement with respect to LeÔŅĹers of Credit to be issued thereaÔŅĹer.  AÔŅĹer the terminaÔŅĹon of an Issuing Lender hereunder, the terminated Issuing Lender shall remain a party hereto and shall conÔŅĹnue to have all the rights and obligaÔŅĹons of an Issuing Lender under this Agreement with respect to any outstanding LeÔŅĹers of Credit issued by it prior to such terminaÔŅĹon. 

(j) Issuing Lender Reports to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent.  Unless otherwise agreed by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, each Issuing Lender shall report in wriÔŅĹng to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent such informaÔŅĹon as the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent shall reasonably request as to the LeÔŅĹers of Credit issued by such Issuing Lender. 

(k) Cash CollateralizaÔŅĹon. If any Event of Default shall occur and be conÔŅĹnuing, on the Business Day that the Borrower receives noÔŅĹce from the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent or the Required Lenders (or, if the maturity of the Loans has been accelerated pursuant to ArÔŅĹcle VIII, Lenders with LC Exposure represenÔŅĹng more than 50% of the total LC Exposure) demanding the deposit of cash collateral pursuant to this paragraph, the Borrower shall immediately deposit into an account established and maintained on the books and records of the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, which account may be a ‚ÄúsecuriÔŅĹes account‚ÄĚ (within the meaning of SecÔŅĹon 8-501 of the UCC), in the name of the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent and for the benefit of the Lenders, an amount in immediately available funds in Dollars equal to 103% of the LC Exposure as of such date plus any accrued and unpaid interest thereon; provided that the obligaÔŅĹon to deposit such cash collateral shall become effecÔŅĹve immediately, and such deposit shall become immediately due and payable, without demand or other noÔŅĹce of any kind, upon the occurrence of any Event of Default with respect to the Borrower described in clause (h) or (i) of ArÔŅĹcle VIII.  The Borrower also shall deposit cash collateral in accordance with this paragraph as and to the extent required by SecÔŅĹon 2.21.  Each such deposit shall be held by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent as collateral for the LC Exposure and other obligaÔŅĹons of the Borrower under this Agreement, and for this purpose the Borrower hereby grants a security interest to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent for the benefit of the Lenders and the Issuing Lenders in such collateral account and in any financial assets (as defined in the UCC) or other property held therein. 

The Administrative Agent shall have exclusive dominion and control, including the exclusive right of withdrawal, over such account.  All amounts on deposit pursuant to this paragraph (l) shall be invested by the Administrative Agent in interest bearing instruments or accounts, with the selection of which instruments or accounts to be determined by the Administrative Agent in its sole discretion; provided that the Administrative Agent shall consult with the Borrower as to the selection of such instruments or accounts; provided further that such investments shall be at the risk and expense of the Borrower.  Other than any interest earned on the investment of such deposits, such deposits shall not bear interest.  Interest or profits, if any, on such investments shall accumulate in such account.  Moneys in such account shall be applied by the Administrative Agent to reimburse the relevant Issuing Lender for LC 

Disbursements for which it has not been reimbursed and, to the extent not so applied, shall be held for the satisfaction of the reimbursement obligations of the Borrower for the LC Exposure at such time or, if the maturity of the Loans has been accelerated (but (i) subject to the consent of Lenders with LC Exposure representing 100% of the total LC Exposure and (ii) in the case of any such application at a time when any Lender is a Defaulting Lender (but only if, after giving effect thereto, the remaining cash collateral shall be less than the aggregate LC Exposure of all the Defaulting Lenders), the consent of each Issuing Lender), be applied to satisfy other obligations of the Borrower under this Agreement.  If the Borrower is required to provide an amount of cash collateral hereunder as a result of the occurrence of an Event of Default, the amount (including any interest and profits earned thereon as aforesaid) standing to the credit of such account (to the extent not applied as aforesaid) shall be returned to the Borrower within three Business Days after all Events of Default have been cured or waived.  If the Borrower is required to provide an amount of cash collateral hereunder pursuant to Section 2.21, such amount (to the extent not applied as aforesaid) shall be returned to the Borrower, as promptly as practicable, to the extent that, after giving effect to such return, no Issuing Lender shall have any exposure in respect of any outstanding Letter of Credit that is not fully covered by the Commitments of the Non-Defaulting Lenders and/or the remaining cash collateral and no Event of Default shall have occurred and be continuing. 

(l) LeÔŅĹer of Credit Amounts. For all purposes of this Agreement, (i) the amount of a LeÔŅĹer of Credit that, by its terms or the terms of any document related thereto, provides for one or more automaÔŅĹc increases in the stated amount thereof shall be deemed to be the maximum stated amount of such LeÔŅĹer of Credit aÔŅĹer giving effect to all such increases (other than any such increase consisÔŅĹng of the reinstatement of an amount previously drawn thereunder and reimbursed), whether or not such maximum stated amount is in effect at the ÔŅĹme of determinaÔŅĹon and (ii) if on any date of determinaÔŅĹon a LeÔŅĹer of Credit has expired by its terms but any amount may sÔŅĹll be drawn thereunder by reason of the operaÔŅĹon of ArÔŅĹcle 29(a) of the Uniform Customs and PracÔŅĹce for Documentary Credits, InternaÔŅĹonal Chamber of Commerce PublicaÔŅĹon No. 600 (or such later version thereof as may be in effect at the applicable ÔŅĹme) or Rule 3.13 or Rule 3.14 of the ISP or similar terms of the LeÔŅĹer of Credit itself, or if compliant documents have been presented but not yet honored, such LeÔŅĹer of Credit shall be deemed to be ‚Äúoutstanding‚ÄĚ and ‚Äúundrawn‚ÄĚ in the amount so remaining available to be paid, and the obligaÔŅĹons of the Borrower and each Lender hereunder shall remain in full force and effect unÔŅĹl the Issuing Lenders and the Lenders shall have no further obligaÔŅĹons to make any payments or disbursements under any circumstances with respect to any LeÔŅĹer of Credit. 

(m) ApplicaÔŅĹon of ISP and UCP. Unless otherwise expressly agreed by an Issuing Lender and the Borrower when a LeÔŅĹer of Credit is issued (including any such agreement applicable to an ExisÔŅĹng LeÔŅĹer of Credit), (i) the rules of the ISP shall apply to each standby LeÔŅĹer of Credit, and (ii) the rules of the Uniform Customs and PracÔŅĹce for Documentary Credits, as most recently published by the InternaÔŅĹonal Chamber of Commerce at the ÔŅĹme of issuance, shall apply to each commercial LeÔŅĹer of Credit. 

(n) LeÔŅĹers of Credit Issued for Account of Others. Notwithstanding that a LeÔŅĹer of Credit (including any ExisÔŅĹng LeÔŅĹer of Credit) issued or outstanding hereunder supports any obligaÔŅĹons of, or is for the account of, any Subsidiary of the Borrower, or states that any such Subsidiary is the ‚Äúaccount party‚ÄĚ, ‚Äúapplicant‚ÄĚ, ‚Äúcustomer‚ÄĚ, ‚ÄúinstrucÔŅĹng party‚ÄĚ or the like of or for such LeÔŅĹer of Credit, and without derogaÔŅĹng from any rights of the applicable Issuing Lender (whether arising by contract, at law, in equity or otherwise) against such Subsidiary in respect of such LeÔŅĹer of Credit, the Borrower (i) shall reimburse, indemnify and compensate the applicable Issuing Lender hereunder for such LeÔŅĹer of Credit (including to reimburse any and all LC Disbursements thereunder, the payment of interest thereon and the payment of fees due under SecÔŅĹon 2.12(b)) as if such LeÔŅĹer of Credit had been issued solely for the account of the Borrower and (ii) irrevocably waives any and all defenses that might otherwise be available to it as a guarantor or surety of any or all of the obligaÔŅĹons of such Subsidiary in respect of such LeÔŅĹer of Credit.  The Borrower hereby acknowledges that the issuance of LeÔŅĹers of Credit for its Subsidiaries inures to the benefit of the Borrower, and that the Borrower‚Äôs business derives substanÔŅĹal benefits from the businesses of its Subsidiaries. 

SECTION 2.07. Funding of Borrowings. Funding by Lenders.  Each Lender shall make each Loan to be made by it hereunder on the proposed date thereof by wire transfer of immediately available funds by 2:00 p.m., New York City time (or, in the case of any Syndicated ABR Loan, 4:00 p.m., New York City time), to the account of the Administrative Agent most recently designated by it for such purpose by notice to the Lenders.  The Administrative Agent will make such Loans available to the Borrower by promptly crediting the amounts so received, in like funds, to an account of the Borrower designated by the Borrower in the applicable Borrowing Request; provided that Syndicated ABR Borrowings made to finance the reimbursement of an LC Disbursement as provided in Section 2.06(f) shall be remitted by the Administrative Agent to the relevant Issuing Lender specified in the applicable Borrowing Request. 

(a) PresumpÔŅĹon by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent. Unless the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent shall have received noÔŅĹce from a Lender prior to the proposed date of any Borrowing that such Lender will not make available to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent such Lender‚Äôs share of such Borrowing, the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent may assume that such Lender has made such share available on such date in accordance with paragraph (a) of this SecÔŅĹon 2.07 and may, in reliance upon such assumpÔŅĹon, make available to the Borrower a corresponding amount.  In such event, if a Lender has not in fact made its share of the applicable Borrowing available to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, then the applicable Lender and the Borrower severally agree to pay to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent forthwith on demand such corresponding amount with interest thereon, for each day from and including the date such amount is made available to the Borrower to but excluding the date of payment to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, at (i) in the case of a payment to be made by such Lender, the greater of the NYFRB Rate and a rate determined by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent in accordance with banking industry rules on interbank compensaÔŅĹon and (ii) in the case of a payment to be made by the Borrower, 

the interest rate applicable to Syndicated ABR Loans.  If the Borrower and such Lender shall pay such interest to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent for the same or an overlapping period, the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent shall promptly remit to the Borrower the amount of such interest paid by the Borrower for such period.  If such Lender pays its share of the applicable Borrowing to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, then the amount so paid shall consÔŅĹtute such Lender‚Äôs Loan included in such Borrowing.  Any payment by the Borrower shall be without prejudice to any claim the Borrower may have against a Lender that shall have failed to make such payment to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent. 

SECTION 2.08. Interest Elections. Elections by the Borrower for Syndicated Borrowings.  The Loans comprising each Syndicated Borrowing initially shall be of the Type specified in the applicable Borrowing Request or as otherwise provided in Section 2.03(d) and, in the case of a Syndicated Term SOFR Borrowing, shall have the Interest Period specified in such Borrowing Request or as otherwise provided in Section 2.03(d).  Thereafter, the Borrower may elect to convert such Syndicated Borrowing to a Borrowing of a different Type or to continue such Borrowing as a Borrowing of the same Type and, in the case of a Syndicated Term SOFR Borrowing, may elect the Interest Period therefor, all as provided in this Section 2.08.  The Borrower may elect different options with respect to different portions of the affected Syndicated Borrowing, in which case each such portion shall be allocated ratably among the Lenders holding the Loans comprising such Borrowing, and the Loans comprising each such portion shall be considered a separate Borrowing.  This Section 2.08 shall not apply to Competitive Borrowings, which may not be converted or continued. 

(a) NoÔŅĹce of ElecÔŅĹons.  To make an elecÔŅĹon pursuant to this SecÔŅĹon 2.08, the Borrower shall noÔŅĹfy the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent of such elecÔŅĹon by telephone by the ÔŅĹme that a Borrowing Request would be required under SecÔŅĹon 2.03 if the Borrower were requesÔŅĹng a Syndicated Borrowing of the Type resulÔŅĹng from such elecÔŅĹon to be made on the effecÔŅĹve date of such elecÔŅĹon.  Each such telephonic Interest ElecÔŅĹon Request shall be irrevocable and shall be confirmed promptly by hand delivery or e-mail (in .pdf or .ÔŅĹf format) to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent of a wriÔŅĹen Interest ElecÔŅĹon Request in a form approved by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent and signed by a Responsible Officer of the Borrower. 

(b) Content of Interest ElecÔŅĹon Requests. Each telephonic and wriÔŅĹen Interest ElecÔŅĹon Request shall specify the following informaÔŅĹon in compliance with SecÔŅĹon 2.02: 

(i) the Borrowing to which such Interest ElecÔŅĹon Request applies and, if different opÔŅĹons are being elected with respect to different porÔŅĹons thereof, the porÔŅĹons thereof to be allocated to each resulÔŅĹng Borrowing (in which case the informaÔŅĹon to be specified pursuant to clauses (iii) and (iv) below shall be specified for each resulÔŅĹng Borrowing); 

(ii) the effecÔŅĹve date of the elecÔŅĹon made pursuant to such Interest ElecÔŅĹon Request, which shall be a Business Day; 

(iii) whether the resulÔŅĹng Borrowing is to be an ABR Borrowing, a Term SOFR Borrowing or, if applicable pursuant to SecÔŅĹon 2.14, a Daily Simple SOFR Borrowing; and 

(iv) if the resulÔŅĹng Borrowing is a Syndicated Term SOFR Borrowing, the Interest Period therefor aÔŅĹer giving effect to such elecÔŅĹon, which shall be a period contemplated by the definiÔŅĹon of the term ‚ÄúInterest Period‚ÄĚ and permiÔŅĹed under SecÔŅĹon 2.02(d). 

If any such Interest Election Request requests a Term SOFR Borrowing but does not specify an Interest Period, then the Borrower shall be deemed to have selected an Interest Period of one month‚Äôs duration. 

(c) NoÔŅĹce by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent to the Lenders.  Promptly following receipt of an Interest ElecÔŅĹon Request, the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent shall advise each Lender of the details thereof and of such Lender‚Äôs porÔŅĹon of each resulÔŅĹng Borrowing. 

(d) Failure to Elect; Events of Default. If the Borrower fails to deliver a ÔŅĹmely and complete Interest ElecÔŅĹon Request with respect to a Syndicated Term SOFR Borrowing prior to the end of the Interest Period therefor, then, unless such Syndicated Term SOFR Borrowing is repaid as provided herein, the Borrower shall be deemed to have selected an Interest Period of one month‚Äôs duraÔŅĹon. 

Notwithstanding any contrary provision hereof, if an Event of Default has occurred and is continuing and the Administrative Agent, at the request of the Required Lenders, so notifies the Borrower (provided that no such notice shall be required in the case of any Event of Default under clause (h) or (i) of Article VII with respect to the Borrower), then, so long as an Event of Default is continuing (A) no outstanding Syndicated Borrowing may be converted to or continued as a Syndicated Term SOFR Borrowing and (B) unless repaid, each Syndicated Term SOFR Borrowing shall be converted to a Syndicated ABR Borrowing at the end of the Interest Period therefor. 

SECTION 2.09. Termination, Reduction and Increase of the Commitments. Scheduled Termination.  Unless previously terminated, each Commitment shall terminate on the Commitment Termination Date applicable to such Commitment. 

(a) Voluntary TerminaÔŅĹon or ReducÔŅĹon. The Borrower may at any ÔŅĹme terminate, or from ÔŅĹme to ÔŅĹme reduce, the Commitments; provided that (i) each parÔŅĹal reducÔŅĹon of the Commitments shall be in an amount that is $5,000,000 or a larger mulÔŅĹple thereof and (ii) the Borrower shall not terminate or reduce the Commitments if, aÔŅĹer giving effect to any concurrent prepayment of the Loans in 

accordance with SecÔŅĹon 2.11, the sum of the total Revolving Credit Exposures plus the aggregate principal amount of outstanding CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve Loans would exceed the total Commitments. 

(b) NoÔŅĹce of Voluntary TerminaÔŅĹon or ReducÔŅĹon. The Borrower shall noÔŅĹfy the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent of any elecÔŅĹon to terminate or reduce the Commitments under paragraph (b) of this SecÔŅĹon 2.09 at least three Business Days prior to the effecÔŅĹve date of such terminaÔŅĹon or reducÔŅĹon, specifying such elecÔŅĹon and the effecÔŅĹve date thereof.  Promptly following receipt of any noÔŅĹce, the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent shall advise the Lenders of the contents thereof.  Each noÔŅĹce delivered by the Borrower pursuant to this SecÔŅĹon 2.09 shall be irrevocable; provided that a noÔŅĹce of terminaÔŅĹon of the Commitments delivered by the Borrower may state that such noÔŅĹce is condiÔŅĹoned upon the occurrence of one or more events set forth therein, in which case such noÔŅĹce may be revoked by the Borrower (by noÔŅĹce to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent on or prior to the specified effecÔŅĹve date) if such condiÔŅĹon is not saÔŅĹsfied. 

(c) Efect of TerminaÔŅĹon or ReducÔŅĹon.  Any terminaÔŅĹon or reducÔŅĹon of the Commitments shall be permanent.  Each reducÔŅĹon of the Commitments shall be made ratably among the Lenders in accordance with their respecÔŅĹve Commitments. 

## (d) Increase of Commitments. 

(i) Requests for Increase. The Borrower may, at any ÔŅĹme following the EffecÔŅĹve Date, effect an increase in the Commitments hereunder (each such increase being a ‚ÄúCommitment Increase‚ÄĚ) by having one or more AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lenders provide new or addiÔŅĹonal Commitments hereunder, by noÔŅĹce to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent specifying the amount of the relevant Commitment Increase, the idenÔŅĹty of the AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lender(s) and the date on which such increase is to be effecÔŅĹve (the ‚ÄúCommitment Increase Date‚ÄĚ), which shall be a Business Day at least three Business Days aÔŅĹer delivery of such noÔŅĹce and 30 days prior to the Commitment TerminaÔŅĹon Date (or, if at such ÔŅĹme, there shall exist different Commitment TerminaÔŅĹon Dates for the Lenders hereunder, the latest applicable Commitment TerminaÔŅĹon Date); provided that: 

(A) the minimum amount of each Commitment Increase shall be $25,000,000; 

(B) immediately aÔŅĹer giving effect to any Commitment Increase, the aggregate Commitments hereunder shall not exceed $1,875,000,000; 

(C) at the ÔŅĹme of any such Commitment Increase, no Default shall have occurred and be conÔŅĹnuing or would result therefrom; and 

(D) the representaÔŅĹons and warranÔŅĹes set forth in ArÔŅĹcle IV and in the other Loan Documents shall be true and correct (x) in the case of the representaÔŅĹons and warranÔŅĹes qualified as to materiality, in all respects and (y) otherwise, in all material respects, in each case on and as of the Commitment Increase Date as if made on and as of such date (or, if any such representaÔŅĹon or warranty is expressly stated to have been made as of a specific date, as of such specific date). 

Each notice by the Borrower under this paragraph shall be deemed to constitute a representation and warranty by the Borrower as to the matters specified in clauses (B), (C) and (D) above as of the relevant Commitment Increase Date.  Notwithstanding anything herein to the contrary, no Lender shall have any obligation hereunder to become an Additional Commitment Lender and any election to do so shall be in the sole discretion of each Lender. 

(ii) EfecÔŅĹveness of Increase.  Each Commitment Increase (and the new or addiÔŅĹonal Commitment of each AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lender resulÔŅĹng therefrom) shall become effecÔŅĹve as of the relevant Commitment Increase Date upon receipt by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, on or prior to 2:00 p.m., New York City ÔŅĹme, on such Commitment Increase Date, of: 

(A) a cerÔŅĹficate executed by a Responsible Officer of the Borrower staÔŅĹng that the condiÔŅĹons with respect to such Commitment Increase under this paragraph (e) have been saÔŅĹsfied; 

(B) an agreement, in form and substance saÔŅĹsfactory to the Borrower and the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, pursuant to which each such AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lender shall, effecÔŅĹve as of such Commitment Increase Date, provide a new or addiÔŅĹonal Commitment hereunder in the amount specified therein and (if not then an exisÔŅĹng Lender) become a Lender hereunder, in each case duly executed by each such AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lender and the Borrower and acknowledged by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent; and 

(C) such evidence of authority of the Borrower to effect such Commitment Increase as the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent may reasonably request. 

Upon the Administrative Agent‚Äôs receipt of a fully executed agreement from each Additional Commitment Lender referred to in clause (B) above, together with the certificates and/or other documents referred to in clauses (A) and (C) above, the Administrative Agent shall record the information contained in each such agreement in the Register and give prompt notice of the effectiveness of the relevant Commitment Increase to the Borrower and the Lenders (including each Additional Commitment Lender), which notice of effectiveness shall be conclusive and binding on the parties hereto. 

(iii) On each Commitment Increase Date, (i) the aggregate principal amount of the Syndicated Loans outstanding (the ‚ÄúExisÔŅĹng Syndicated Borrowings‚ÄĚ) immediately prior to the effecÔŅĹveness of such  Commitment Increase shall be deemed to be repaid, (ii) each AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lender that shall have had a Commitment prior to the effecÔŅĹveness of such Commitment Increase shall pay to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent in Dollars, in immediately available funds, an amount equal to the difference between (A) the product of (1) such Lender‚Äôs Applicable Percentage (calculated aÔŅĹer giving ResulÔŅĹng Syndicated Borrowings, (iv) aÔŅĹer the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent receives the funds specified in clauses (ii) and (iii) above, the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent shall pay to each Lender the porÔŅĹon of such funds that is equal to the difference between (A) the product of (1) such Lender‚Äôs Applicable Percentage (calculated without giving effect to the effecÔŅĹveness of such Commitment Increase) mulÔŅĹplied by (2) the aggregate amount of the ExisÔŅĹng Syndicated Borrowings, and (B) the product of (1) such Lender‚Äôs Applicable Percentage (calculated aÔŅĹer giving effect to the effecÔŅĹveness of such Commitment Increase) mulÔŅĹplied by (2) the aggregate amount of the ResulÔŅĹng Syndicated Borrowings, (v) aÔŅĹer the effecÔŅĹveness of such  Commitment Increase, the Borrower shall be deemed to have made new Syndicated Borrowings (the ‚ÄúResulÔŅĹng Syndicated Borrowings‚ÄĚ) in an aggregate amount equal to the aggregate amount of the ExisÔŅĹng Syndicated Borrowings and of the Types and for shall pay each Lender any and all accrued but unpaid interest on its Loans comprising the ExisÔŅĹng Syndicated Borrowings.  The deemed payments of the ExisÔŅĹng Syndicated Borrowings made pursuant to clause (i) above shall be subject to compensaÔŅĹon by the Borrower pursuant to the provisions of SecÔŅĹon 2.16 if the date of the effecÔŅĹveness of such Commitment Increase occurs other than on the last day of the Interest Period relaÔŅĹng thereto.  Upon each Commitment Increase, the parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹon interests of the Lenders in the then outstanding LeÔŅĹers of Credit shall automaÔŅĹcally be adjusted to reflect, 

and each Lender (including each AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lender) shall have a parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹon in each such LeÔŅĹer of Credit equal to, the Lenders‚Äô respecÔŅĹve Applicable Percentage of the aggregate amount available to be drawn under each such LeÔŅĹer of Credit, aÔŅĹer giving effect to such Commitment Increase. 

SECTION 2.10. Repayment of Loans; Evidence of Debt. Repayment. 

The Borrower hereby unconditionally promises to pay the Loans as follows: 

(i) to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent for account of each Lender the outstanding principal amount of the Syndicated Loans of such Lender on the Commitment TerminaÔŅĹon Date applicable to such Syndicated Loans, and 

(ii) to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent for account of each Lender the then unpaid principal amount of each CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve Loan of such Lender on the last day of the Interest Period therefor. 

(e) Maintenance of Records by Lenders. Each Lender shall maintain in accordance with its usual pracÔŅĹce records evidencing the indebtedness of the Borrower to such Lender resulÔŅĹng from each Loan made by such Lender, including the amounts of principal and interest payable and paid to such Lender from ÔŅĹme to ÔŅĹme hereunder. 

(f) Maintenance of Records by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent. The AdministraÔŅĹve Agent shall maintain records in which it shall record (i) the amount of each Loan made hereunder, the Class and Type thereof and, if applicable, each Interest Period therefor, (ii) the amount of any principal or interest due and payable or to become due and payable from the Borrower to each Lender hereunder and (iii) the amount of any sum received by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent hereunder for account of the Lenders and each Lender‚Äôs share thereof. 

(g) Efect of Entries.  The entries made in the records maintained pursuant to paragraph (b) or (c) of this SecÔŅĹon 2.10 shall be prima facie evidence of the existence and amounts of the obligaÔŅĹons recorded therein; provided that the failure of any Lender or the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent to maintain such records or any error therein shall not in any manner affect the obligaÔŅĹon of the Borrower to repay the Loans or pay any other amounts hereunder in accordance with the terms of this Agreement. 

(h) Promissory Notes.  Any Lender may request that Loans made by it be evidenced by a promissory note.  In such event, the Borrower shall prepare, execute and deliver to such Lender a promissory note payable to such Lender and its registered assigns and in customary form reasonably saÔŅĹsfactory to the Borrower and the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent.  ThereaÔŅĹer, the Loans evidenced by such promissory note and interest thereon shall at all ÔŅĹmes (including aÔŅĹer assignment pursuant to SecÔŅĹon 10.04) be represented by one or more promissory notes in such form payable to the payee named therein or its registered assigns. 

SECTION 2.11. Prepayment of Loans. Optional Prepayments.  The Borrower shall have the right at any time and from time to time to prepay any Borrowing in whole or in part, without premium or penalty, subject to the requirements of this Section 2.11; provided that the Borrower shall not have the right to prepay any Competitive Loan without the prior consent of the Lender thereof. 

(a) NoÔŅĹces, Etc. The Borrower shall noÔŅĹfy the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent by telephone (confirmed by hand delivery or e-mail (in .pdf or .ÔŅĹf format)) of any prepayment hereunder (i) in the case of prepayment of a Syndicated Term SOFR Borrowing or of a CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve Borrowing, not later than 12:00 noon, New York City ÔŅĹme, three Business Days before the date of prepayment, (ii) in the case of prepayment of a Syndicated Daily Simple SOFR Borrowing, 1:00 p.m., New York City ÔŅĹme, five U.S. Government SecuriÔŅĹes Business Days before the date of prepayment or (iii) in the case of prepayment of a Syndicated ABR Borrowing, not later than 12:00 noon, New York City ÔŅĹme, on the date of prepayment.  Each such noÔŅĹce shall be irrevocable and shall specify the prepayment date and the principal amount of each Borrowing or porÔŅĹon thereof to be prepaid; provided that a noÔŅĹce of prepayment delivered by the Borrower may state that such noÔŅĹce is condiÔŅĹoned upon the occurrence of one or more events set forth therein, in which case such noÔŅĹce of prepayment may be revoked by the Borrower (by noÔŅĹce to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent on or prior to the specified effecÔŅĹve date) if such condiÔŅĹon is not saÔŅĹsfied.  Promptly following receipt of any such noÔŅĹce relaÔŅĹng to a Syndicated Borrowing or CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve Borrowing, the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent shall advise the Lenders of the contents thereof.  Each parÔŅĹal prepayment of any Borrowing shall be in an amount that would be permiÔŅĹed in the case of a Borrowing of the same Class and Type as provided in SecÔŅĹon 2.02.  Each prepayment of a Borrowing shall be applied ratably to the Loans included in the prepaid Borrowing.  Prepayments shall be accompanied by accrued interest to the extent required by SecÔŅĹon 2.13 and any payments pursuant to SecÔŅĹon 2.16, if applicable.  If the Borrower provides a noÔŅĹce of prepayment of Syndicated Loans but fails to make a ÔŅĹmely selecÔŅĹon of the Syndicated Borrowing or Syndicated Borrowings to be prepaid, such prepayment shall be applied, first, to any outstanding Syndicated ABR Borrowings, second, to the outstanding Syndicated Daily Simple SOFR Borrowings, and, third, to the outstanding Syndicated Term SOFR Borrowings in the order of the remaining duraÔŅĹon of their respecÔŅĹve Interest Periods (the Borrowing with the shortest remaining Interest Period to be repaid first). 

SECTION 2.12. Fees. Facility Fees.  The Borrower agrees to pay to the Administrative Agent for account of each Lender a facility fee, which shall accrue at the Applicable Rate on the daily amount of the Commitment of such Lender (whether used or unused) during the period from and including the date hereof to but excluding the date such Commitment terminates; provided that if such Lender continues to have any Revolving Credit Exposure after its Commitment terminates, then such facility fee shall continue to accrue on the daily amount of such Lender‚Äôs Revolving Credit Exposure from and including the date on which its Commitment terminates to but excluding the date on which such Lender ceases to have any Revolving Credit Exposure.  Facility fees accrued 

through and including each Quarterly Date shall be payable on the 15th Business Day following such Quarterly Date and on the date the Commitments terminate, commencing on the first such date to occur after the date hereof; provided that all facility fees shall be payable on the date on which the Commitments terminate and any facility fees accruing after the date on which the Commitments terminate shall be payable on demand.  All facility fees shall be computed on the basis of a year of 360 days and shall be payable for the actual number of days elapsed (including the first day but excluding the last day). 

(a) LeÔŅĹer of Credit Fees. The Borrower agrees to pay (i) to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent for account of each Lender a parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹon fee with respect to its parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹons in LeÔŅĹers of Credit, which shall accrue at a rate per annum equal to the Applicable Rate applicable to interest on Syndicated Term SOFR Loans (or, the case of Documentary LeÔŅĹers of Credit, 50% of such Applicable Rate) on the average daily amount of such Lender‚Äôs LC Exposure (excluding any porÔŅĹon thereof aÔŅĹributable to unreimbursed LC Disbursements) during the period from and including the EffecÔŅĹve Date to but excluding the later of the date on which such Lender‚Äôs Commitment terminates and the date on which such Lender ceases to have any LC Exposure, and (ii) to each Issuing Lender a fronÔŅĹng fee, which shall accrue at the rate or rates per annum separately agreed upon between the Borrower and such Issuing Lender on the average daily amount of the LC Exposure (excluding any porÔŅĹon thereof aÔŅĹributable to unreimbursed LC Disbursements) in respect of LeÔŅĹers of Credit issued by such Issuing Lender during the period from and including the EffecÔŅĹve Date to but excluding the later of the date of terminaÔŅĹon of the Commitments and the date on which there ceases to be any such LC Exposure, as well as such Issuing Lender‚Äôs standard fees with respect to the administraÔŅĹon, issuance, amendment or extension of any LeÔŅĹer of Credit or processing of drawings thereunder.  ParÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹon fees and fronÔŅĹng fees accrued through and including each Quarterly Date shall be payable on the 15th Business Day following such Quarterly Date, commencing on the first such date to occur aÔŅĹer the EffecÔŅĹve Date; provided that all such fees shall be payable on the date on which the Commitments terminate and any such fees accruing aÔŅĹer the date on which the Commitments terminate shall be payable on demand.  Any other fees payable to any Issuing Lender pursuant to this paragraph shall be payable within 10 days aÔŅĹer demand.  All parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹon fees and fronÔŅĹng fees shall be computed on the basis of a year of 360 days and shall be payable for the actual number of days elapsed (including the first day but excluding the last day). 

(b) AdministraÔŅĹve Agent Fees. The Borrower agrees to pay to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, for its own account, fees payable in the amounts and at the ÔŅĹmes separately agreed upon between the Borrower and the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent. 

(c) Payment of Fees.  All fees payable hereunder shall be paid on the dates due, in Dollars and immediately available funds, to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent (or to the relevant Issuing Lender, in the case of fees payable to it) for distribuÔŅĹon, in the case of facility fees and parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹon fees, to the Lenders enÔŅĹtled thereto.  Fees paid shall not be refundable under any circumstances. 

SECTION 2.13. Interest. ABR Loans.  The Loans comprising each ABR Borrowing shall bear interest at a rate per annum equal to the Alternate Base Rate plus the Applicable Rate. 

(a) Term SOFR Loans. The Loans comprising each Term SOFR Borrowing shall bear interest at a rate per annum equal to (i) in the case of a Syndicated Term SOFR Borrowing, the Adjusted Term SOFR for the Interest Period for such Borrowing plus the Applicable Rate, or (ii) in the case of a CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve Term SOFR Borrowing, the Adjusted Term SOFR for the Interest Period for such Borrowing plus (or minus, as applicable) the Margin applicable to such Borrowing. 

(b) Daily Simple SOFR Loans. The Loans comprising each Daily Simple SOFR Borrowing (if such Type of Borrowing is applicable pursuant to SecÔŅĹon 2.14) shall bear interest at a rate per annum equal to the Adjusted Daily Simple SOFR plus the Applicable Rate. 

(c) Fixed Rate Loans.  Each Fixed Rate Loan shall bear interest at a rate per annum equal to the Fixed Rate applicable to such Loan. 

(d) Default Interest.  Notwithstanding the foregoing, if any principal of or interest on any Loan or any fee or other amount payable by the Borrower hereunder is not paid when due, whether at stated maturity, upon acceleraÔŅĹon or otherwise, such overdue amount shall bear interest, aÔŅĹer as well as before judgment, at a rate per annum equal to (i) in the case of overdue principal of any Loan, 2% plus the rate otherwise applicable to such Loan as provided above or (ii) in the case of any other amount, 2% plus the rate applicable to ABR Loans as provided in paragraph (a) of this SecÔŅĹon 2.13. 

(e) Payment of Interest.  Accrued interest on each Loan shall be payable in arrears on each Interest Payment Date for such Loan and, in the case of Syndicated Loans, upon terminaÔŅĹon of the Commitments; provided that (i) interest accrued pursuant to paragraph (e) of this SecÔŅĹon 2.13 shall be payable on demand; (ii) in the event of any repayment or prepayment of any Loan (other than a prepayment of a Syndicated ABR Loan prior to the Commitment TerminaÔŅĹon Date applicable to such Loan), accrued interest on the principal amount repaid or prepaid shall be payable on the date of such repayment or prepayment; and (iii) in the event of any conversion of any Syndicated Term SOFR Borrowing prior to the end of the Interest Period therefor, accrued interest on such Borrowing shall be payable on the effecÔŅĹve date of such conversion. 

(f) ComputaÔŅĹon.  All interest hereunder shall be computed on the basis of a year of 360 days, except that interest computed by reference to the Alternate Base Rate at ÔŅĹmes when the Alternate Base Rate is based on the Prime Rate shall be computed on the basis of a year of 365 days (or 366 days in a leap year), and in each case shall be payable for the actual number of days elapsed (including the first day but 

excluding the last day).  The applicable Alternate Base Rate, Adjusted Term SOFR or Adjusted Daily Simple SOFR shall be determined by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, and such determinaÔŅĹon shall be conclusive absent manifest error.

SECTION 2.15. Increased Costs. Increased Costs Generally.  If any 

Change in Law shall: 

(i) impose, modify or deem applicable any reserve, special deposit, compulsory loan, insurance charge or similar requirement against assets of, deposits with or for the account of, or credit extended or parÔŅĹcipated in by, any Lender or any Issuing Lender;

and the result of any of the foregoing shall be to increase the cost to such Lender of making, converting to, continuing or maintaining any Loan (or of maintaining its obligation to make any such Loan) or to increase the cost to such Lender or such Issuing 

Lender of participating in, issuing or maintaining any Letter of Credit (or of maintaining its obligation to participate in or to issue any Letter of Credit), or to reduce the amount of any sum received or receivable by such Lender or such Issuing Lender or the Administrative Agent hereunder (whether of principal, interest or any other amount) then, upon request of such Lender, such Issuing Lender or the Administrative Agent, as the case may be, the Borrower will pay to such Lender, such Issuing Lender or the Administrative Agent, as the case may be, in Dollars, such additional amount or amounts as will compensate such Lender, such Issuing Lender or the Administrative Agent, as the case may be, for such additional costs or expense incurred or reduction suffered. 

(h) Capital and Liquidity Requirements.  If any Lender or any Issuing Lender determines that any Change in Law affecÔŅĹng such Lender or such Issuing Lender or any lending office of such Lender or such Issuing Lender or such Lender‚Äôs or such Issuing Lender‚Äôs holding company, if any, regarding capital or liquidity requirements has had or would have the effect of reducing the rate of return on such Lender‚Äôs or such Issuing Lender‚Äôs capital or on the capital of such Lender‚Äôs or such Issuing Lender‚Äôs holding company, if any, as a consequence of this Agreement, the Commitment of such Lender or the Loans made by, or parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹons in LeÔŅĹers of Credit held by, such Lender, or the LeÔŅĹers of Credit issued by such Issuing Lender, to a level below that which such Lender or such Issuing Lender or such Lender‚Äôs or such Issuing Lender‚Äôs holding company could have achieved but for such Change in Law (taking into consideraÔŅĹon such Lender‚Äôs or such Issuing Lender‚Äôs policies and the policies of such Lender‚Äôs or such Issuing Lender‚Äôs holding company with respect to capital adequacy and liquidity), then from ÔŅĹme to ÔŅĹme the Borrower will pay to such Lender or such Issuing Lender, as the case may be, in Dollars, such addiÔŅĹonal amount or amounts as will compensate such Lender or such Issuing Lender or such Lender‚Äôs or such Issuing Lender‚Äôs holding company for any such reducÔŅĹon suffered. 

(i) CerÔŅĹfcates for Reimbursement.  A cerÔŅĹficate of a Lender or an Issuing Lender seÔŅĹng forth the amount or amounts in Dollars (and including a reasonable statement as to the calculaÔŅĹon of such amount or amounts) necessary to compensate such Lender or such Issuing Lender or its holding company, as the case may be, as specified in paragraph (a) or (b) of this SecÔŅĹon 2.15 and delivered to the Borrower shall be conclusive absent manifest error.  The Borrower shall pay such Lender or such Issuing Lender, as the case may be, the amount shown as due on any such cerÔŅĹficate within 10 days aÔŅĹer receipt thereof. 

(j) Delay in Requests. Failure or delay on the part of any Lender or any Issuing Lender to demand compensaÔŅĹon pursuant to this SecÔŅĹon 2.15 shall not consÔŅĹtute a waiver of such Lender‚Äôs or such Issuing Lender‚Äôs right to demand such compensaÔŅĹon, provided that the Borrower shall not be required to compensate a Lender or an Issuing Lender pursuant to this SecÔŅĹon 2.15 for any increased costs incurred or reducÔŅĹons suffered more than nine months prior to the date that such Lender or such Issuing Lender, as the case may be, noÔŅĹfies the Borrower of the Change in Law giving rise to such increased costs or reducÔŅĹons and of such Lender‚Äôs or such 

Issuing Lender‚Äôs intenÔŅĹon to claim compensaÔŅĹon therefor (except that, if the Change in Law giving rise to such increased costs or reducÔŅĹons is retroacÔŅĹve, then the nine-month period referred to above shall be extended to include the period of retroacÔŅĹve effect thereof). 

(k) CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve Loans. Notwithstanding the foregoing provisions of this SecÔŅĹon 2.15, a Lender shall not be enÔŅĹtled to compensaÔŅĹon pursuant to this SecÔŅĹon 2.15 in respect of any CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve Loan if the Change in Law (other than any Change in Law referred to in the proviso of the definiÔŅĹon of such term) that would otherwise enÔŅĹtle it to such compensaÔŅĹon shall have been publicly announced prior to submission of the CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve Bid pursuant to which such Loan was made. 

SECTION 2.16. Break Funding Payments. In the event of (a) the payment of any principal of any Term SOFR Loan or Fixed Rate Loan other than on the last day of the Interest Period applicable thereto (including as a result of an Event of Default), (b) the conversion or continuation of any Syndicated Term SOFR Loan other than on the last day of the Interest Period therefor, (c) the failure to borrow, convert, continue or prepay any Syndicated Loan on the date specified in any notice delivered pursuant hereto (regardless of whether such notice is permitted to be revocable under Section 2.11(b) or 2.14(a) and is revoked in accordance therewith), (d) the failure to borrow any Competitive Loan after accepting the Competitive Bid to make such Loan, or (e) the assignment as a result of a request by the Borrower pursuant to Section 2.19(b) of any Syndicated Term SOFR Loan other than on the last day of the Interest Period applicable thereto, then, in any such event, the Borrower shall compensate each Lender for the loss, cost and expense attributable to such event.  A certificate of any Lender setting forth any amount or amounts that such Lender is entitled to receive pursuant to this Section 2.16 shall be delivered to the Borrower and shall be conclusive absent manifest error.  The Borrower shall pay such Lender the amount shown as due on any such certificate within 10 days after receipt thereof. 

SECTION 2.17. Taxes. Payments Free of Taxes. Any and all payments by or on account of any obligation of the Borrower or any Subsidiary Guarantor hereunder or under any other Loan Document shall be made free and clear of and without deduction or withholding for any Indemnified Taxes (including Other Taxes); provided that if the Borrower or any Subsidiary Guarantor shall be required by applicable law to deduct any Indemnified Taxes (including any Other Taxes) from such payments, then (i) the sum payable shall be increased as necessary so that after making all required deductions (including deductions applicable to additional sums payable under this Section 2.17) the Administrative Agent or Lender, as the case may be, receives an amount equal to the sum it would have received had no such deductions been made, (ii) the Borrower or such Subsidiary Guarantor shall make or cause to be made such deductions and (iii) the Borrower or such Subsidiary Guarantor shall timely pay or cause to be paid the full amount deducted to the relevant Governmental Authority in accordance with applicable law. 

(a) Payment of Other Taxes by the Borrower. Without limiÔŅĹng the provisions of paragraph (a) above, the Borrower and each Subsidiary Guarantor shall ÔŅĹmely pay any Other Taxes to the relevant Governmental Authority in accordance with applicable law. 

(b) IndemnifcaÔŅĹon by the Borrower. The Borrower shall indemnify the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent and each Lender, within 30 days aÔŅĹer wriÔŅĹen demand therefor, for the full amount of any Indemnified Taxes (including Other Taxes and Indemnified Taxes imposed or asserted on or aÔŅĹributable to amounts paid or payable under this SecÔŅĹon 2.17, but excluding Excluded Taxes under all circumstances) paid or payable by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent or such Lender, as the case may be, and any penalÔŅĹes and interest  arising therefrom or with respect thereto, whether or not such Indemnified Taxes (including Other Taxes) were correctly or legally imposed or asserted by the relevant Governmental Authority.  A cerÔŅĹficate as to the amount of such payment or liability, prepared in good faith and delivered to the Borrower by a Lender (with a copy to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent), or by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent on its own behalf or on behalf of a Lender, shall be conclusive absent manifest error.  The Borrower shall not be obligated to indemnify for any Indemnified Taxes (including Other Taxes) if a wriÔŅĹen demand therefor is not made by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent or a Lender, as the case may be, within 120 days from the first date the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent or such Lender, as the case may be, knows or reasonably should have known of the imposiÔŅĹon of such Taxes. 

(c) Evidence of Payments. As soon as pracÔŅĹcable aÔŅĹer any payment of Indemnified Taxes (including Other Taxes) by the Borrower or any Subsidiary Guarantor to a Governmental Authority, the Borrower or such Subsidiary Guarantor shall deliver to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent the original or a cerÔŅĹfied copy of a receipt issued by such Governmental Authority evidencing such payment or other evidence of such payment reasonably saÔŅĹsfactory to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent. 

(d) IndemnifcaÔŅĹon by the Lenders.  Each Lender shall severally indemnify the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent for any Taxes aÔŅĹributable to such Lender (but only to the extent that the Borrower and the Subsidiary Guarantors have not already indemnified the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent for such Taxes and without limiÔŅĹng the obligaÔŅĹon of the Borrower and the Subsidiary Guarantors to do so) that are paid or payable by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent in connecÔŅĹon with any Loan Document and any reasonable expenses arising therefrom or with respect thereto, whether or not such Taxes were correctly or legally imposed or asserted by the relevant Governmental Authority.  The indemnity under this paragraph (e) shall be paid within 10 days aÔŅĹer the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent delivers to the applicable Lender a cerÔŅĹficate staÔŅĹng the amount of Taxes so paid or payable by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent.  Such cerÔŅĹficate shall be conclusive of the amount so paid or payable absent manifest error. 

(e) Lender Tax CerÔŅĹfcaÔŅĹons.     Any Lender that is enÔŅĹtled to an exempÔŅĹon from, or reducÔŅĹon of, any applicable withholding Tax with respect to any payments under any Loan Document shall deliver to the Borrower and the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, at the ÔŅĹme or ÔŅĹmes reasonably requested by the Borrower or the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, such properly completed and executed documentaÔŅĹon reasonably requested by the Borrower or the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent as will permit such payments to be made without, or at a reduced rate of, withholding. Notwithstanding anything to the contrary in the preceding two sentences, the compleÔŅĹon, execuÔŅĹon and submission of such documentaÔŅĹon (other than such documentaÔŅĹon set forth in SecÔŅĹon 2.17(f)(ii)(A), 2.17(f)(ii)(B) or 2.17(f)(ii)(D)) shall not be required if in the Lender‚Äôs reasonable judgment such compleÔŅĹon, execuÔŅĹon or submission would subject such Lender to any material unreimbursed cost or expense or would materially prejudice the legal or commercial posiÔŅĹon of such Lender. SECTION 2.18. Payments Generally; Pro Rata Treatment; Sharing of Setoffs. Payments by the Obligors.  Each Obligor shall make each payment required to be made by it hereunder (whether of principal, interest, fees or reimbursement of LC Disbursements, or of amounts payable under Section 2.15, 2.16 or 2.17, or otherwise), or under any other Loan Document (except to the extent otherwise provided therein), prior to 1:00 p.m., New York City time, on the date when due, in immediately available funds, without setoff or counterclaim.  Any amounts received after such time on any date may, in the discretion of the Administrative Agent, be deemed to have been received on the next succeeding Business Day for purposes of calculating interest thereon.  All such payments shall be made to the Administrative Agent at the Administrative Agent‚Äôs Account, except as otherwise expressly provided in the relevant Loan Document and except payments to be made directly to an Issuing Lender as expressly provided herein and except payments pursuant to Sections 2.15, 2.16, 2.17 and 10.03, which shall be made directly to the Persons entitled thereto.  The Administrative Agent shall distribute any such payments received by it for account of any other Person to the appropriate recipient promptly following receipt thereof.  If any payment hereunder shall be due on a day that is not a Business Day, the date for payment shall be extended to the next succeeding Business Day and, in the case of any payment accruing interest, interest thereon shall be payable for the period of such extension.  All payments under each Loan Document shall be made in Dollars. 

(a) ApplicaÔŅĹon of Insufcient Payments. If at any ÔŅĹme insufficient funds are received by and available to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent to pay fully all amounts 

of principal, unreimbursed LC Disbursements, interest and fees then due hereunder, such funds shall be applied (i) first, to pay all fees then due, and all costs and expenses then due or reimbursable, to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, in its capacity as such, under any Loan Document, (ii) second, to reimburse all unreimbursed LC Disbursements and to pay all leÔŅĹer of credit fronÔŅĹng fees then due hereunder, ratably between the Issuing Lenders enÔŅĹtled thereto in accordance with the amounts thereof then due to the Issuing Lenders, (iii) third, to pay all other interest and other fees then due hereunder, ratably among the parÔŅĹes enÔŅĹtled thereto in accordance with the amounts of such interest and fees then due to such parÔŅĹes, and (iv) fourth, to pay all other principal then due hereunder, ratably among the parÔŅĹes enÔŅĹtled thereto in accordance with the amounts of such principal then due to such parÔŅĹes. 

(b) Pro Rata Treatment. Except to the extent otherwise provided herein (for the avoidance of doubt, as this Agreement is in effect from ÔŅĹme to ÔŅĹme), including SecÔŅĹons 2.09(e)(iii), 2.20(d) and 2.21: (i) each payment of facility fees under SecÔŅĹon 2.12(a) and leÔŅĹer of credit parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹon fees under SecÔŅĹon 2.12(b) shall be made for account of the Lenders, and each terminaÔŅĹon or reducÔŅĹon of the amount of the Commitments under SecÔŅĹon 2.09 shall be applied to the respecÔŅĹve Commitments of the Lenders, pro rata according to the amounts of their respecÔŅĹve Commitments (or, in the case of any such payment of facility fees or leÔŅĹer of credit parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹon fees at a ÔŅĹme when the Commitments shall have terminated or expired, pro rata according to the amounts of their respecÔŅĹve Revolving Credit Exposure or LC Exposure, as applicable); (ii) each Syndicated Borrowing shall be allocated pro rata among the Lenders according to the amounts of their respecÔŅĹve Commitments (in the case of the making of Syndicated Loans) or their respecÔŅĹve Loans that are to be included in such Borrowing (in the case of conversions and conÔŅĹnuaÔŅĹons of Syndicated Loans); and (iii) each payment or prepayment of any Syndicated Borrowing shall be applied ratably to the Loans included in the repaid or prepaid Syndicated Borrowing. 

(c) Sharing of Payments by Lenders.  If any Lender shall, by exercising any right of setoff or counterclaim or otherwise, obtain payment in respect of any principal of or interest on any of its Loans (other than a CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve Loan) or parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹons in LC Disbursements resulÔŅĹng in such Lender‚Äôs receiving payment of a greater proporÔŅĹon of the aggregate amount of its Loans (other than CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve Loans) and accrued interest thereon than the proporÔŅĹon received by any other Lender, then the Lender receiving such greater proporÔŅĹon shall (i) noÔŅĹfy the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent of such fact and (ii) purchase (for cash at face value) parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹons in the Loans (other than CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve Loans) and parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹons in LC Disbursements of other Lenders, or make such other adjustments as shall be equitable, so that the benefit of all such payments shall be shared by the Lenders ratably in accordance with the aggregate amounts of principal of and accrued interest on their Loans (other than CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve Loans) and parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹons in LC Disbursements, provided that: 

(i) if any such parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹons are purchased and all or any porÔŅĹon of the payment giving rise thereto is recovered, such parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹons shall be rescinded and the purchase price restored to the extent of such recovery, without interest; and 

(ii) the provisions of this paragraph shall not be construed to apply to (x) any payment made by any Obligor pursuant to and in accordance with the express terms of this Agreement (for the avoidance of doubt, as this Agreement is in effect from ÔŅĹme to ÔŅĹme), including SecÔŅĹons 2.09(e)(iii), 2.20(d) and 2.21, or (y) any payment obtained by a Lender as consideraÔŅĹon for the assignment of or sale of a parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹon in any of its Loans or parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹons in LC Disbursements to any Eligible Assignee. 

Each Obligor consents to the foregoing and agrees, to the extent it may effectively do so under applicable law, that any Lender acquiring a participation pursuant to the foregoing arrangements may exercise against each Obligor rights of setoff and counterclaim with respect to such participation as fully as if such Lender were a direct creditor of each Obligor in the amount of such participation. 

(d) Payments by the Borrower; PresumpÔŅĹons by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent. Unless the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent shall have received noÔŅĹce from the Borrower prior to the date on which any payment is due to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent for the account of the Lenders or an Issuing Lender hereunder that the Borrower will not make such payment, the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent may assume that the Borrower has made such payment on such date in accordance herewith and may, in reliance upon such assumpÔŅĹon, distribute to the Lenders or such Issuing Lender, as the case may be, the amount due.  In such event, if the Borrower has not in fact made such payment, then each of the Lenders or such Issuing Lender, as the case may be, severally agrees to repay to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent forthwith on demand the amount so distributed to such Lender or such Issuing Lender with interest thereon, for each day from and including the date such amount is distributed to it to but excluding the date of payment to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, at the greater of the NYFRB Rate and a rate determined by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent in accordance with banking industry rules on interbank compensaÔŅĹon. 

(e) Certain DeducÔŅĹons by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent.  If any Lender shall fail to make any payment required to be made by it hereunder to or for the account of the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent or any Issuing Lender, then the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent may, in its discreÔŅĹon (notwithstanding any contrary provision hereof), (i) apply any amounts thereaÔŅĹer received by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent for the account of such Lender to saÔŅĹsfy such Lender‚Äôs obligaÔŅĹons in respect of such payment unÔŅĹl all such unsaÔŅĹsfied obligaÔŅĹons have been discharged or (ii) hold any such amounts in a segregated account as cash collateral for, and applicaÔŅĹon to, any future funding obligaÔŅĹons of such Lender pursuant to this Agreement (including pursuant to 

SecÔŅĹons 2.06(e), 2.06(f), 2.07(b), 2.18(e) and 10.03(c)), in each case in such order as shall be determined by the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent in its discreÔŅĹon. 

SECTION 2.19. Mitigation Obligations; Replacement of Lenders. Designation of a Different Lending Office. If any Lender requests compensation under Section 2.15, or requires the Borrower to pay any additional amount to any Lender or any Governmental Authority for the account of any Lender pursuant to Section 2.17, then such Lender shall use reasonable efforts to designate a different lending office for funding or booking its Loans hereunder or to assign and delegate its rights and obligations hereunder to another of its offices, branches or Affiliates, if, in the judgment of such Lender, such designation or assignment and delegation (i) would eliminate or reduce amounts payable pursuant to Section 2.15 or 2.17, as the case may be, in the future and (ii) would not subject such Lender to any unreimbursed cost or expense and would not otherwise be disadvantageous to such Lender.  The Borrower hereby agrees to pay all reasonable costs and expenses incurred by any Lender in connection with any such designation or assignment and delegation. 

(a) Replacement of Lenders. If (i) any Lender requests compensaÔŅĹon under SecÔŅĹon 2.15, (ii) the Borrower is required to pay any addiÔŅĹonal amount to any Lender or any Governmental Authority for the account of any Lender pursuant to SecÔŅĹon 2.17, (iii) any Lender has become a DefaulÔŅĹng Lender, (iv) any Lender has become a Non-Extending Lender or (v) any Lender does not consent to any proposed amendment, supplement, modificaÔŅĹon, consent or waiver of any provision of this Agreement or any other Loan Document that requires the consent of such Lender or each of the Lenders or each of the Lenders affected thereby (so long as the consent of the Required Lenders has been obtained), then the Borrower may, at its sole expense and effort, upon noÔŅĹce to such Lender and the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, require such Lender to assign and delegate, without recourse (in accordance with and subject to the restricÔŅĹons contained in, and consents required by, SecÔŅĹon 10.04), all of its interests, rights (other than its exisÔŅĹng rights to payment pursuant to SecÔŅĹon 2.15 or 2.17) and obligaÔŅĹons under this Agreement and the related Loan Documents (other than any outstanding CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve Loans held by it) to an Eligible Assignee that shall assume such obligaÔŅĹons (which assignee may be another Lender, if a Lender accepts such assignment), provided that: 

(A) the Borrower shall have received the prior wriÔŅĹen consent of the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent (and, if a Commitment or any Lender‚Äôs obligaÔŅĹons in respect of LC Exposure is being assigned, each Issuing Lender), which consent shall not unreasonably be withheld; 

(B) the Borrower shall have paid to the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent the assignment fee specified in SecÔŅĹon 10.04; 

(C) such Lender shall have received payment of an amount equal to the outstanding principal of its Loans (other than CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve 

Loans) and parÔŅĹcipaÔŅĹons in LC Disbursements that have been funded by such Lender, accrued interest thereon, accrued fees and all other amounts (except CompeÔŅĹÔŅĹve Loans) payable to it hereunder and under the other Loan Documents (including any amounts under SecÔŅĹon 2.16) from the assignee (to the extent of such outstanding principal and accrued interest and fees) or the Borrower (in the case of all other amounts); 

(D) in the case of any such assignment and delegaÔŅĹon resulÔŅĹng from a claim for compensaÔŅĹon under SecÔŅĹon 2.15 or payments required to be made pursuant to SecÔŅĹon 2.17, such assignment and delegaÔŅĹon will result in a reducÔŅĹon in such compensaÔŅĹon or payments thereaÔŅĹer; 

(E) in the case of any such assignment and delegaÔŅĹon resulÔŅĹng from any Lender becoming a Non-Extending Lender, the assignee shall be an AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lender and, upon the effecÔŅĹveness of any such assignment and delegaÔŅĹon, such assignee shall be deemed to have consented to the extension of the Commitment TerminaÔŅĹon Date requested in the relevant Extension Request (and, if such assignment and delegaÔŅĹon shall become effecÔŅĹve aÔŅĹer the relevant Extension Closing Date, the Commitment TerminaÔŅĹon Date with respect to such AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lender (insofar as relaÔŅĹng to the interests, rights and obligaÔŅĹons under this Agreement and the related Loan Documents so assigned and delegated) shall automaÔŅĹcally extend to the date specified in the relevant Extension Request); and 

(F) such assignment does not conflict with applicable law. 

A Lender shall not be required to make any such assignment or delegation if, prior thereto, as a result of a waiver by such Lender or otherwise, the circumstances entitling the Borrower to require such assignment and delegation cease to apply.  Each party hereto agrees that an assignment and delegation required pursuant to this paragraph may be effected pursuant to an Assignment and Assumption executed by the Borrower, the Administrative Agent and the assignee and that the Lender required to make such assignment and delegation need not be a party thereto. 

SECTION 2.20. Extension of Commitment Termination Date. The Borrower may, by notice to the Administrative Agent (which shall promptly notify the Lenders) not more than 90 days and not less than 30 days prior to each anniversary of the date hereof (or if such anniversary date is not a Business Day, the Business Day next succeeding such anniversary), request (each, an ‚ÄúExtension Request‚ÄĚ) that the Lenders extend, effective on such anniversary date, the Commitment Termination Date then in effect (or, if at such time there shall exist different Commitment Termination Dates for the Lenders hereunder, the latest applicable Commitment Termination Date then in effect) (the ‚ÄúExisting Commitment Termination Date‚ÄĚ) for an additional one year (the 

date on which the closing with respect to any such Extension Request shall occur is referred to herein as an ‚ÄúExtension Closing Date‚ÄĚ); provided that only two Extension Requests may be requested hereunder.  Each Lender, acting in its sole discretion, shall, by notice to the Borrower and the Administrative Agent given not later than the 20th day (or such later day as shall be acceptable to the Borrower) following the date of the Borrower‚Äôs notice, advise the Borrower and the Administrative Agent whether or not such Lender agrees to such extension; provided that any Lender that does not so advise the Borrower shall be deemed to have rejected such Extension Request (any such Lender which shall have rejected or is deemed to have rejected such extension being a ‚ÄúNon-Extending Lender‚ÄĚ).  The election of any Lender to agree to such extension shall not obligate any other Lender to so agree.  Notwithstanding anything herein to the contrary, no Lender shall have any obligation hereunder to extend its Commitment. 

(a) The Borrower shall have the right, at any ÔŅĹme on or prior to, or at any ÔŅĹme following, the relevant Extension Closing Date, unless an Event of Default shall have occurred and be conÔŅĹnuing, to replace any Non-Extending Lender with one or more AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lenders in accordance with SecÔŅĹon 2.19(b).  If requested by the Borrower or the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, each such AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lender shall enter into an agreement with the Borrower and the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, in form and substance saÔŅĹsfactory to the Borrower and the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent, pursuant to which such AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lender shall reconfirm its Commitment hereunder so assumed from the relevant Non-Extending Lender and, in the case of any such replacement becoming effecÔŅĹve aÔŅĹer the relevant Extension Closing Date, reconfirm the extension of the Commitment TerminaÔŅĹon Date applicable thereto as contemplated by clause (E) of SecÔŅĹon 2.19(b). 

(b) If (and only if) the total of the Commitments of the Lenders that have agreed in connecÔŅĹon with any Extension Request to extend the ExisÔŅĹng Commitment TerminaÔŅĹon Date and (if applicable) the Commitments of the AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lender(s) that shall have replaced any Non-Extending Lender as contemplated by paragraph (b) above shall, in the aggregate, be at least 50% of the aggregate amount of the Commitments in effect immediately prior to the Extension Closing Date, then, subject to the occurrence of the Extension Closing Date, effecÔŅĹve as of the Extension Closing Date, the Commitment TerminaÔŅĹon Date, but only with respect to each Lender that has agreed to so extend its Commitment and (if applicable) each AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lender that has replaced a Non-Extending Lender (and to Commitments and Loans of each such Lender and AddiÔŅĹonal Commitment Lender), shall be extended to the date that is one year aÔŅĹer the then ExisÔŅĹng Commitment TerminaÔŅĹon Date (or, if such date is not a Business Day, the immediately preceding Business Day); provided that the occurrence of the Extension Closing Date and the effecÔŅĹveness of the extension of the ExisÔŅĹng Commitment TerminaÔŅĹon Date shall not become effecÔŅĹve with respect to any Lender unless as of the Extension Closing Date: (i) no Default shall have occurred and be conÔŅĹnuing; (ii) the representaÔŅĹons and warranÔŅĹes of the Obligors set forth in ArÔŅĹcle IV and in the other Loan Documents shall be true and correct (A) in the case of the representaÔŅĹons and warranÔŅĹes qualified as to 

materiality, in all respects and (B) otherwise, in all material respects, in each case on and as of the Extension Closing Date as if made on and as of such date (or, if any such representaÔŅĹon or warranty is expressly stated to have been made as of a specific date, as of such specific date); and (iii) the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent shall have received a cerÔŅĹficate executed by a Responsible Officer of the Borrower, dated as of the Extension Closing Date, staÔŅĹng that the condiÔŅĹons with respect to such extension have been saÔŅĹsfied.  Upon the occurrence of the Extension Closing Date, the AdministraÔŅĹve Agent shall record the relevant informaÔŅĹon in the Register and give prompt noÔŅĹce of such occurrence to the Borrower and the Lenders, which noÔŅĹce shall be conclusive and binding. 

(c) Notwithstanding anything herein to the contrary, (i) with respect to any Non-Extending Lender, the Commitment TerminaÔŅĹon Date for such Lender shall remain unchanged (and the Commitment of such Commitments and (ii) the ‚ÄúAvailability Period‚ÄĚ and the ‚ÄúCommitment TerminaÔŅĹon Date‚ÄĚ (without taking into consideraÔŅĹon any extension pursuant to this SecÔŅĹon 2.20), as such terms are used
